using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Xml;

public class XmlConfigurationParser
{
    public Dictionary<string, string> ParseXmlConfiguration(string xmlFilePath)
    {
        var settings = new Dictionary<string, string>();
        
        var xmlReaderSettings = new XmlReaderSettings
        {
            DtdProcessing = DtdProcessing.Parse,
            ValidationType = ValidationType.DTD,
            XmlResolver = new XmlUrlResolver(),
            IgnoreWhitespace = true,
            IgnoreComments = true
        };

        using (var reader = XmlReader.Create(xmlFilePath, xmlReaderSettings))
        {
            while (reader.Read())
            {
                if (reader.NodeType == XmlNodeType.Element && reader.Name == "setting")
                {
                    string key = reader.GetAttribute("key");
                    string value = reader.GetAttribute("value");
                    
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(key))
                    {
                        settings[key] = value ?? string.Empty;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        return settings;
    }

    public Dictionary<string, string> ParseXmlConfigurationFromString(string xmlContent)
    {
        var settings = new Dictionary<string, string>();
        
        var xmlReaderSettings = new XmlReaderSettings
        {
            DtdProcessing = DtdProcessing.Parse,
            ValidationType = ValidationType.DTD,
            XmlResolver = new XmlUrlResolver(),
            IgnoreWhitespace = true,
            IgnoreComments = true
        };

        using (var stringReader = new StringReader(xmlContent))
        using (var reader = XmlReader.Create(stringReader, xmlReaderSettings))
        {
            while (reader.Read())
            {
                if (reader.NodeType == XmlNodeType.Element && reader.Name == "setting")
                {
                    string key = reader.GetAttribute("key");
                    string value = reader.GetAttribute("value");
                    
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(key))
                    {
                        settings[key] = value ?? string.Empty;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        return settings;
    }

    public Dictionary<string, string> ParseXmlConfigurationUsingXmlDocument(string xmlFilePath)
    {
        var settings = new Dictionary<string, string>();
        
        var xmlDoc = new XmlDocument();
        xmlDoc.XmlResolver = new XmlUrlResolver();
        xmlDoc.Load(xmlFilePath);
        
        XmlNodeList settingNodes = xmlDoc.SelectNodes("//setting");
        
        if (settingNodes != null)
        {
            foreach (XmlNode node in settingNodes)
            {
                if (node.Attributes != null)
                {
                    string key = node.Attributes["key"]?.Value;
                    string value = node.Attributes["value"]?.Value;
                    
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(key))
                    {
                        settings[key] = value ?? string.Empty;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        return settings;
    }

    public Dictionary<string, string> ParseXmlConfigurationFromStream(Stream xmlStream)
    {
        var settings = new Dictionary<string, string>();
        
        var xmlReaderSettings = new XmlReaderSettings
        {
            DtdProcessing = DtdProcessing.Parse,
            ValidationType = ValidationType.DTD,
            XmlResolver = new XmlUrlResolver(),
            IgnoreWhitespace = true,
            IgnoreComments = true
        };

        using (var reader = XmlReader.Create(xmlStream, xmlReaderSettings))
        {
            while (reader.Read())
            {
                if (reader.NodeType == XmlNodeType.Element && reader.Name == "setting")
                {
                    string key = reader.GetAttribute("key");
                    string value = reader.GetAttribute("value");
                    
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(key))
                    {
                        settings[key] = value ?? string.Empty;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        return settings;
    }

    public Dictionary<string, object> ParseNestedXmlConfiguration(string xmlFilePath)
    {
        var settings = new Dictionary<string, object>();
        
        var xmlDoc = new XmlDocument();
        xmlDoc.XmlResolver = new XmlUrlResolver();
        xmlDoc.Load(xmlFilePath);
        
        XmlNode root = xmlDoc.DocumentElement;
        
        if (root != null)
        {
            ParseNode(root, settings);
        }
        
        return settings;
    }

    private void ParseNode(XmlNode node, Dictionary<string, object> settings)
    {
        foreach (XmlNode child in node.ChildNodes)
        {
            if (child.NodeType == XmlNodeType.Element)
            {
                if (child.Attributes != null && child.Attributes.Count > 0)
                {
                    var attributes = new Dictionary<string, string>();
                    foreach (XmlAttribute attr in child.Attributes)
                    {
                        attributes[attr.Name] = attr.Value;
                    }
                    settings[child.Name] = attributes;
                }
                else if (child.HasChildNodes && child.FirstChild.NodeType == XmlNodeType.Text)
                {
                    settings[child.Name] = child.InnerText;
                }
                else if (child.HasChildNodes)
                {
                    var nestedSettings = new Dictionary<string, object>();
                    ParseNode(child, nestedSettings);
                    settings[child.Name] = nestedSettings;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package main

import (
	"encoding/xml"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"strings"
)

type Configuration struct {
	XMLName  xml.Name  `xml:"configuration"`
	Settings []Setting `xml:"settings>setting"`
	Database Database  `xml:"database"`
	Server   Server    `xml:"server"`
}

type Setting struct {
	Key   string `xml:"key,attr"`
	Value string `xml:",chardata"`
}

type Database struct {
	Host     string `xml:"host"`
	Port     int    `xml:"port"`
	Username string `xml:"username"`
	Password string `xml:"password"`
	Name     string `xml:"name"`
}

type Server struct {
	Host    string `xml:"host"`
	Port    int    `xml:"port"`
	Timeout int    `xml:"timeout"`
	SSL     bool   `xml:"ssl"`
}

func ParseXMLConfig(xmlData io.Reader) (*Configuration, error) {
	decoder := xml.NewDecoder(xmlData)
	decoder.Strict = false
	decoder.Entity = xml.HTMLEntity

	var config Configuration
	err := decoder.Decode(&config)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse XML: %w", err)
	}

	return &config, nil
}

func ParseXMLConfigFromString(xmlString string) (*Configuration, error) {
	return ParseXMLConfig(strings.NewReader(xmlString))
}

func main() {
	xmlConfig := `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<configuration>
    <settings>
        <setting key="app_name">MyApplication</setting>
        <setting key="version">1.0.0</setting>
        <setting key="debug">true</setting>
    </settings>
    <database>
        <host>localhost</host>
        <port>5432</port>
        <username>admin</username>
        <password>secret&amp;pass</password>
        <name>mydb</name>
    </database>
    <server>
        <host>0.0.0.0</host>
        <port>8080</port>
        <timeout>30</timeout>
        <ssl>false</ssl>
    </server>
</configuration>`

	config, err := ParseXMLConfigFromString(xmlConfig)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing XML: %v\n", err)
		return
	}

	fmt.Printf("Configuration parsed successfully:\n")
	fmt.Printf("Settings:\n")
	for _, setting := range config.Settings {
		fmt.Printf("  %s: %s\n", setting.Key, setting.Value)
	}
	fmt.Printf("\nDatabase:\n")
	fmt.Printf("  Host: %s\n", config.Database.Host)
	fmt.Printf("  Port: %d\n", config.Database.Port)
	fmt.Printf("  Username: %s\n", config.Database.Username)
	fmt.Printf("  Password: %s\n", config.Database.Password)
	fmt.Printf("  Name: %s\n", config.Database.Name)
	fmt.Printf("\nServer:\n")
	fmt.Printf("  Host: %s\n", config.Server.Host)
	fmt.Printf("  Port: %d\n", config.Server.Port)
	fmt.Printf("  Timeout: %d\n", config.Server.Timeout)
	fmt.Printf("  SSL: %t\n", config.Server.SSL)
}
